# Reasoning Patterns

Durable reasoning patterns distilled from completed sessions. The post-task chain appends entries when reflection output includes pattern fields or extractable bullets.

## Required fields (each entry)

- **Problem type:** What class of situation triggered the friction or mistake
- **What worked:** Reasoning approach or fix that resolved it
- **What failed:** Approach that failed and why
- **When to apply:** Triggers for reusing this pattern in future sessions

## Template

```markdown
### PATTERN-YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS: [Short title]

- Session ID:
- Problem type:
- What worked:
- What failed:
- When to apply:
- Verification evidence:
```

## Entries

### PATTERN-20260601-224343: Ralph verify failures from inline shell quoting, not missing code

- Session ID: 2b1dc119-2d70-4d39-89f0-63d880cebf61
- Problem type: Ralph loop reports repeated verify failure (shell EOF / exit 2) while the feature under test is already built and a standalone verify script passes.
- What worked: Treat verify script exit 0 as ground truth for implementation completeness, then inspect `harness/memory/ralph-goal.md` for a truncated or mangled `verify_command`. Normalize storage to a script path (`sh harness/scripts/verify-gnu-packet-modules.sh`) instead of inline nested-quote shell. Use harness-workflow decomposition for the feature work; use a dedicated verify script for Ralph persistence.
- What failed: Storing a long inline verify string with nested single quotes (e.g. `grep -v '^0$'`) directly in `ralph-goal.md`. The stored command was truncated at `grep -v '^0`, causing unclosed-quote shell EOF on Ralph iterations 12–17 despite `verify-gnu-packet-modules.sh` exiting 0 with 8 JAR class matches.
- When to apply: Any Ralph goal or harness memory ledger that persists shell verify commands; especially commands containing single quotes, pipes, subshells, or Gradle/jar pipelines. When Ralph iterations fail with shell syntax/EOF errors but a project verify script passes manually.
- Verification evidence: `sh harness/scripts/verify-gnu-packet-modules.sh` exit 0 (8 entries); rollout ROLLOUT-20260601-WF-PKT-001; post-task chain generation `2b1dc119-retry` graded PENDING-20260601-RALPH-VERIFY at 81/100; Ralph iterations 12–17 failed with documented truncated `grep -v '^0` in ralph-goal.md.

### PATTERN-20260601-224913: End-to-end verify post-task adapter without treating no_proposal as failure

- Session ID: cmd-verify
- Problem type: Need to end-to-end verify post-task adapter long-session behavior (output_tokens threshold, background SDK chain) without treating expected no_proposal outcomes as harness failures.
- What worked: Drive post-task-adapter.sh from verify-harness-commands.sh with a fixed synthetic payload (`{"session_id":"cmd-verify","output_tokens":1500}`). Assert foreground invariants only: parseable JSON and absence of HARNESS_POSTTASK_AUTO_CHAIN. Let the background SDK chain run and log rollouts; treat gate=no_proposal with proposal=null as success when the session is an infrastructure smoke test with no transcript or deliverables.
- What failed: Interpreting gate=no_proposal or skipped grading as a failed harness run during verify-script smoke tests. The self-test path is designed to exercise wiring, not to surface durable improvement proposals.
- When to apply: When changing post-task hooks, output_tokens thresholds, post-task-adapter.sh, or SDK background orchestration; when extending verify-harness-commands.sh with end-to-end post-task coverage; when distinguishing infrastructure verification sessions from real user sessions that should yield proposals.
- Verification evidence: Ported from linux minecraft thing and .cursor-harness harness memory; verify-harness-commands.sh post-task section; post-task-chain.log cmd-verify tokens=1500 gate=no_proposal.

### PATTERN-20260602-225155: Anticheat Invalid packets on multi-hit combat with a lag module queui...

- Session ID: 066a859f-e5a4-497b-a8ce-87ea7c175e8b
- Problem type: Anticheat Invalid packets on multi-hit combat with a lag module queuing outbound C03 — stale pre-knockback movement burst-sent after server S12 velocity, causing position desync and weak-KB feel.
- What worked: User clarification that KnockbackDelay was off narrowed blame to Lagrange. Compare Raven LagRange/UnifiedLagHandler semantics; distinguish cancelLagQueue (drop stale C03 without sending) from flushQueueNow (ordered intentional release); cancel on self S12/S19/hurt in onReceive immediately, not on the next tick; keep flushQueueNow for range/distance/attack-drain paths only.
- What failed: Calling flushQueueNow on hurt tick (and related hurt/airborne guards) — burst-sent every queued C03 from before knockback after S12 had already been applied, producing Invalid packets (3) and apparent weak knockback.
- When to apply: Fake-lag/LagRange modules queuing outbound movement (especially C03-only queues); Vulcan Invalid packets on hits or multi-hit chains; user reports weak KB with lag modules but velocity/kbdelay modules disabled; any lag module that flushes on hurtTime without checking whether queued packets predate knockback.
- Verification evidence: ./gradlew shadowJar BUILD SUCCESSFUL; gnu-client.jar copied to GNUClient/install/lib/; harness/reports/rollout-log.md ROLLOUT-20260602-WF-LAGRANGE-HIT-INVALID-005; LagrangeModule.java contains cancelLagQueue(), abortLagNow(), and onReceive S12/S19 cancel paths (inferred from repo state; transcript excerpt not provided).

### PATTERN-20260602-225449: Post-task hook background SDK chain starts in post-task-chain.log but...

- Session ID: setsid-verify-1780430011
- Problem type: Post-task hook background SDK chain starts in post-task-chain.log but never reaches done — child node process killed when the hook shell exits because it shares the hook process group.
- What worked: Launch node post-task-chain.js via setsid when available (nohup fallback) inside a subshell, then background with `&` and append to post-task-chain.log. Use a traceable synthetic session_id (setsid-verify-*) and output_tokens >= 1000 to exercise the long-session path; assert foreground JSON invariants only and let the detached chain complete reflection in the background.
- What failed: Backgrounding node with `&` alone within the hook subshell without setsid/nohup — the child remains tied to the hook process group and is torn down when the hook exits, producing log lines with start but no done.
- When to apply: When modifying .cursor/hooks/post-task-adapter.sh or any Cursor hook that spawns long-running background orchestration; when post-task-chain.log shows start without matching done; when validating fixes for background chain truncation after hook return.
- Verification evidence: harness/reports/post-task-chain.log line 198: start generation=setsid-verify-1780430011 tokens=1500 cursor=set obsidian=set. .cursor/hooks/post-task-adapter.sh lines 96-123: setsid (nohup fallback) wraps background node post-task-chain.js with explicit comment that hook process-group teardown otherwise kills the child. output_tokens 1500 >= THRESHOLD 1000 triggers run_sdk_chain().

### PATTERN-20260602-225850: Anticheat flags and disconnects from (a) queuing Netty transaction co...

- Session ID: 6637b8ce-82dd-4757-8bef-cb328c31b855
- Problem type: Anticheat flags and disconnects from (a) queuing Netty transaction confirm packets (C0F/S32) in lag/backtrack modules, and (b) sprint modules re-asserting sprint while serverSprintState is already true or re-enabling sprint immediately on attack instead of vanilla one-tick delay.
- What worked: Centralize protocol-critical packet exemptions in PacketHelper and return false (pass-through) before any module queue. For sprint: gate setSprintKeyState on !McAccess.getServerSprintState() (field_175171_bO); remove direct sendSprintActionPacket; remove onSend/attack handler so only onTickStart re-presses the keybind after vanilla cancels sprint on hit. Resolve user path typos (player/ vs movement/) via glob/read without blocking.
- What failed: Direct sendSprintActionPacket and immediate attack-handler setSprintKeyState caused duplicate or mistimed C0B (Vulcan BadPackets, Grim simulation). Per-module exemption lists without PacketHelper missed S32 on Backtrack inbound. setSprinting(true) each tick (earlier session context) desyncs server/client sprint state.
- When to apply: GNUClient or 1.8.9 client modules using Lagrange/Blink/Backtrack/KnockbackDelay queues—always exempt keepalive, chat, and transaction confirm packets centrally. When anticheat reports BadPackets Entity Action or sprint simulation flags: read serverSprintState before sprint actions, use keybind not manual C0B, and preserve vanilla one-tick re-sprint delay after attacks (tick handler only, no packet listener).
- Verification evidence: ./gradlew shadowJar BUILD SUCCESSFUL on each one-pass iteration; gnu-client.jar copied to GNUClient/install/lib/gnu-client.jar. SprintModule.java final state: onTickStart gates setSprintKeyState on !McAccess.getServerSprintState(); no PacketListener/onSend/sendSprintActionPacket. PacketHelper adds isClientConfirmTransaction/isServerConfirmTransaction and extends outbound/inbound exempt helpers.

### PATTERN-20260602-230123: World-space visual overlays (ESP, tracers, nametags) misaligned or in...

- Session ID: 3fd00a9f-d9f9-4d3d-8ebe-75a2b604b697
- Problem type: World-space visual overlays (ESP, tracers, nametags) misaligned or invisible in injected obfuscated 1.8.9 GNUClient because RenderManager viewerPosX/Y/Z reflection reads return 0.0 (wrong field names); tick-cached viewer position from those fields is also invalid.
- What worked: Add McAccess.renderViewEntity() with deobf getRenderViewEntity plus func_175606_aa SRG fallback; McAccess.getViewerPos(mc, partialTicks) interpolates render-view entity last/pos coordinates. Call getViewerPos once per onRender frame in each visual module; keep entity enumeration and field reads in onTick cache only (no reflection in render loop). Remove broken viewerPosX/Y/Z/viewerCoord helpers. Verify with ./gradlew shadowJar and ESP debug log showing non-zero vp=.
- What failed: Reading RenderManager field_78730_l/m/n (viewerPos) and field_78728_j/k/l (renderPos) via reflection — all returned 0.0 in the live injected runtime, producing overlays offset from the camera.
- When to apply: GNUClient or JVMTI-injected 1.8.9 clients rendering world-space boxes, tracers, nametags, or bed ESP during RenderWorldLastEvent; when overlays cluster at wrong world coordinates or vp debug logs show 0,0,0; whenever McAccess camera anchor is needed and RenderManager static viewer fields cannot be trusted.
- Verification evidence: ./gradlew shadowJar BUILD SUCCESSFUL; gnu-client.jar copied to GNUClient/install/lib/; EspModule onRender calls McAccess.getViewerPos(mc, partialTicks) and logs ESP debug vp= with non-zero values (inferred from agent transcript 6637b8ce lines 954–961 and current repo state; direct transcript for session 3fd00a9f not on disk). post-task-chain.log line 121 records start generation=3fd00a9f tokens=3806; no matching done line — retro replay via 3fd00a9f-retro.

### PATTERN-20260602-230149: Post-task SDK chain logged start without done for a substantive user ...

- Session ID: 65239e03-d238-49e2-aced-c19a683e1fbe
- Problem type: Post-task SDK chain logged start without done for a substantive user session, and agent transcript file is missing — reflection must infer from harness logs only.
- What worked: Use post-task-chain.log start/done pairing to identify incomplete generations; queue substantive sessions (tokens >= 3000) through harness/scripts/retroactive-reflect.sh with a -retro generation-id to bypass dedup; locate transcripts via find "$CURSOR_TRANSCRIPTS_DIR" -name "${sessionId}.jsonl"; treat same-day workflow rollouts as circumstantial context only when session IDs are absent.
- What failed: Assuming the original background node chain completed because cursor=set was logged, or attempting detailed deliverable reconstruction without a transcript. Relying on any done rollout= line after a -retro start to mark completion — post-task-chain.log line 211 starts 65239e03-retro while line 216 done belongs to session 6637b8ce, causing a false already-completed skip in retroactive-reflect.log.
- When to apply: When post-task-chain.log shows start generation=<uuid> without a matching done or reasoning pattern appended for that session; when batch-processing incomplete sessions for a date via retroactive-reflect.sh; when find_transcript returns empty for a real user session; when diagnosing June-2026-era chains that predate or bypass setsid detachment in post-task-adapter.sh.
- Verification evidence: harness/reports/post-task-chain.log line 120: start generation=65239e03-d238-49e2-aced-c19a683e1fbe tokens=9158 cursor=set obsidian=set (no matching done rollout= or reasoning pattern appended for this session). find "$TRANSCRIPT_DIR" -name 65239e03*.jsonl returned empty. harness/reports/retroactive-reflect.log queued session for -retro replay. PATTERN-20260602-225449 documents pre-setsid hook process-group kill as root cause for start-without-done on 2026-06-02.

### PATTERN-20260602-230323: Vulcan anticheat flags AimAssist on vertical pitch speed/uniformity; ...

- Session ID: 6637b8ce-82dd-4757-8bef-cb328c31b855
- Problem type: Vulcan anticheat flags AimAssist on vertical pitch speed/uniformity; mouse-GCD-based pitch cap produces near-zero steps in injected runtime; lag-module packet queuing and sprint re-assertion cause BadPackets/Invalid packets; post-task SDK chain child killed when hook shell exits.
- What worked: Separate verticalSpeed default (~40% horizontal) with fixed maxPitchStep = v * 0.15f (not GCD). Layer humanization: exponential easeFactor(1-exp(-ang/8)), sin-phase correlated jitter, per-axis speed lerp, probabilistic skip-ticks (15% yaw / 10% pitch), overshoot correction under 3°, GCD rounding on final steps. For lag/sprint: centralize transaction/keepalive/chat exemptions in PacketHelper; cancel stale C03 on knockback not flush; gate sprint on !serverSprintState via keybind only. For harness: spawn post-task-chain.js with setsid (nohup fallback) so background chain survives hook return; retroactive-reflect.sh filters by tokens, done lines, and in-progress -retro runs.
- What failed: maxPitchStep = verticalSpeed * getMouseSensitivityGcd() yielded ~0 because GCD factor is near-zero in injected context — pitch cap effectively disabled rotation. Lagrange 1-packet/tick + 50ms gap stagger was reverted; user preferred instant full drain on Lagrange while keeping stagger only on Blink. flushQueueNow on hurt tick burst-sent pre-knockback C03 causing weak KB and Invalid packets (addressed in earlier session turns). Retroactive-reflect first pass incorrectly skipped in-progress -retro runs and had prefix-match bugs matching original IDs to -retro starts.
- When to apply: When Vulcan or similar AC flags AimAssist on pitch uniformity or speed; when proposing rotation caps in injected clients — prefer fixed speed multipliers over live mouse GCD. When humanizing aim: stack easing, correlated jitter, skip-ticks, and overshoot rather than white noise alone. When lag/backtrack modules queue movement packets and AC reports Invalid/BadPackets on hits or block place. When post-task-chain.log shows start without done after hook return. When batch-replaying reflections, guard dedup with exact generation ID matching and track in-progress -retro suffix runs.
- Verification evidence: ./gradlew shadowJar BUILD SUCCESSFUL on each one-pass iteration; gnu-client.jar copied to GNUClient/install/lib/gnu-client.jar. AimAssistModule.java final state: verticalSpeed default 1.2f, maxPitchStep = v * 0.15f, easeFactor with EASE_REACH 8.0f, sin-phase jitter (JITTER_AMP 0.018f), 15%/10% skip-tick gates, yawOvershot correction, speed lerp (SPEED_LERP_ALPHA 0.20f), roundGcd on steps. setsid-verify-1780430011 test session: post-task-chain.log shows start generation with matching done within minutes. retroactive-reflect.sh created at harness/scripts/retroactive-reflect.sh with MIN_TOKENS=3000, --generation-id X-retro dedup bypass, 10s pause between runs; June 2 batch started after fixing prefix-match and in-progress completion detection bugs.

### PATTERN-20260602-230843: Post-task SDK chain logged start without done for a substantive user ...

### PATTERN-20260603-005125: Anticheat flags aim-assist rotation as too fast or too uniform; an in...

- Session ID: 6637b8ce-82dd-4757-8bef-cb328c31b855
- Problem type: Anticheat flags aim-assist rotation as too fast or too uniform; an initial pitch cap tied to live mouse sensitivity GCD collapsed to ~0 at runtime, negating the cap.
- What worked: Replace GCD-dependent pitch cap with an explicit speed-proportional constant (`verticalSpeed * 0.15f`, parallel to horizontal `* 0.1f`). Layer humanization incrementally from user specs: separate vertical speed, fixed cap, then speed jitter, probabilistic skip ticks, and small-angle overshoot — one pass plus rebuild per feedback cycle.
- What failed: Using `McAccess.getMouseSensitivityGcd()` (OpenMyau RotationUtil formula on `field_74320_O`) as the per-tick pitch step cap multiplier. Despite a correct reference implementation, the runtime product `verticalSpeed × GCD` was near-zero, so pitch was effectively uncapped and still flagged.
- When to apply: When tuning combat aim/rotation modules for anticheat (Vulcan-style uniformity/speed checks). When a sensitivity- or GCD-derived multiplier produces unexpectedly tiny step caps at runtime. When user reports one axis is too fast or too robotic — fix caps with explicit speed scales first, then add stochastic humanization layers.
- Verification evidence: Each pass ran `./gradlew shadowJar` successfully and copied `GNUClient/client/build/libs/gnu-client.jar` to `GNUClient/install/lib/gnu-client.jar`. Pass 2 removed GCD from pitch cap (`maxPitchStep = v * 0.15f`). Pass 3 added yawOvershot state, speed jitter, and probabilistic skip-tick gates; assistant confirmed implementation before the next user query.

- Problem type: Grim anticheat flags persist on a ported fake-lag module even after combat state machine matches raven-bS — symptoms oscillate between PostTimer, Simulation, BadPacketsX, PacketOrderB/F, and rubberbanding as release strategy changes.
- What worked: Treat each Grim flag as a wire-order symptom, not a slider-tuning problem. Read raven-bS UnifiedLagHandler and LagRange: single outbound FIFO (movement + actions delayed together), flushLag ends the session without synchronous full drain, expired packets release on tick-start, drain continues on next send/tick pass, combat logic before movement packets (PrePlayerInteract not tick END), Lagrange listener registered last (LOWEST). Remove all synthetic C03 paths (catch-up, resync C04, pre-attack injection, staggered drain). For jump/KB exits use flushQueueNow (FIFO send) on normal ground leave; reserve cancelLagQueue only for velocity/hurt.
- What failed: C03-only queue while exempting C0A/C0B/C0F/C0F-transactions — splits live actions from stale positions. Gradual 1–2 C03/tick release while vanilla sends every tick — BadPacketsX double-movement. Hold-only lag with no release — extreme rubberband. Burst flushQueueNow/drainMovementQueueNow immediately before C02 attack — PacketOrderB pre-attack and AntiKB. Staggered/spread release at high delay (309ms) — worsened desync vs Raven batch age release. Assuming slider reduction (122ms, 0.5 desync) fixes structural packet-order bugs.
- When to apply: Porting or debugging 1.8.9 Grim-sensitive Lagrange/FakeLag/Blink/Backtrack modules in GNUClient or similar injected clients. When user reports Simulation/PacketOrder/BadPackets despite 'logic parity' with Raven. When considering C03-only delay vs action exempt lists. Before adding any synthetic movement packet (catch-up, resync, pre-attack inject).
- Verification evidence: Transcript 6637b8ce: 2640 lines, 4341 tool calls, 10050 output tokens. Repeated `./gradlew shadowJar` / `compileJava` BUILD SUCCESSFUL with jar staged to GNUClient/install/lib/gnu-client.jar. User on velocity dummy: BadPackets fixed; later 'progress!!! we are now flagging really less no more simulation flags'. Harness: HARNESS_RETRO_SELFTEST=1 retroactive-reflect.sh exit 0; doctor-meta-readiness.sh milestone 3 PASS (3/3 USER-PREF after CRLF fix); curation apply verification grep/du checks passed. - Problem type: Grim/Vulcan anticheat flags persist on a ported Lagrange module after combat-logic and release-rate tuning — root cause is split outbound exempt list (live C0A/C0B/C0F while C03 queued) breaking wire packet order versus raven-bS UnifiedLagHandler.

Tuning delay/desync sliders without auditing exempt-vs-queued split. Diagnosing Backtrack when user's Grim repro was Lagrange-only.
